***цапля.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:цапля.html>ца́пля</a> (21943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čapľa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цапля.html>ца́пля</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cáplja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цапля.html>ца́пли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цапля.html>ца́пли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цапля.html>ца́пель</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ца́пелька</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heron, egret <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">bird</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> beanpole, a tall, thin person (<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>)</li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a></i>, <i>ts</i> (in the Russian phonetic spelling alphabet)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царапать.html>цара́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">carápatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царапнуть.html>цара́пнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поцарапать.html>поцара́пать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оцарапать.html>оцара́пать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нацарапать.html>нацара́пать</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:царевич.html>царе́вич</a> (13791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-евич</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evič</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царевич.html>царе́вич</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">carévič</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царевич.html>царе́вича</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царевич.html>царе́вичи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царевич.html>царе́вичей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царевна.html>царе́вна</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tsarevich (son of a tsar, a prince in Russia or Bulgaria)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***царить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:царить.html>цари́ть</a> (5542)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царить.html>цари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">carítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">воцари́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be a tsar (monarch), to reign = <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствовать.html>ца́рствовать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">cárstvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>to reign, to dominate, to prevail</li></ol>

***царица.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́ца</a> (8146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">caríca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́ц</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tsarina, tsaritsa</li>
<li>empress, queen (in ancient or Non-European monarchies)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́ца</a></b> са́вская</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>caríca</b> Sávskaja</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Queen_of_Sheba" class="extiw" title="w:Queen of Sheba">Queen of Sheba</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> queen</li></ol>

***царствие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:царствие.html>ца́рствие</a> (22316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствие.html>ца́рствие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cárstvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствие.html>ца́рствия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствие.html>ца́рствия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствие.html>ца́рствий</a></b>)
</p>

***царствование.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:царствование.html>ца́рствование</a> (21053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствовать.html>ца́рствовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cárstvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствование.html>ца́рствование</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cárstvovanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствование.html>ца́рствования</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствование.html>ца́рствования</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царствование.html>ца́рствований</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tsardom, kingdom, reign, ruling, governing (of an emperor)</li></ol>

***царь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a> (1131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">цьсарь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cĭsarĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">цѣсарь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cěsarĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*cěsařь</i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> language, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kaisaraz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Caesar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">carʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царя́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>цари́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царе́й</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́ца</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tsar, Russian emperor</li>
<li>king (figuratively, or referring to ancient or Non-European monarchs)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>звере́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>carʹ</b> zveréj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">king of beasts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>carʹ</b> i box</i> ― <span class="e-translation">God Almighty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:небесный.html>небе́сный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>carʹ</b> nebésnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Heavenly Father</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></b> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царе́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>carʹ</b> <b>caréj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">King of kings</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царе́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́хе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pri <b>caré</b> Goróxe</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the year dot; a very long time ago; since the beginning</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голове́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On bez carjá v golové!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He’s stupid!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>From 1721 to 1917, Russia was officially an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_Empire" class="extiw" title="w:Russian Empire">Empire</a>, and its monarchs referred to as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:император.html>импера́тор</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imperátor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (officially), <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государь.html>госуда́рь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gosudárʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самодержец.html>самоде́ржец</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samodéržec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; for much of that time period, referring to the Russian monarch as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> was seen as a colloquialism.</li></ul>

***цвести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:цвести.html>цвести́</a> (8571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kvisti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвести.html>цвести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cvestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расцвести.html>расцвести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bloom, to blossom, to flower</li>
<li>to flourish, to prosper</li>
<li><i>water</i> to become overgrown, to be covered with duckweed/mold</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выцвета́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vycvetátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">доцвета́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">docvetátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зацветать.html>зацвета́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zacvetátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отцветать.html>отцвета́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otcvetátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>(no equivalent)</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a> (896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*květъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱweyt-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">white</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">white</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cvet</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цве́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвета́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цвето́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>colour</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cvet</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цве́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цвето́в</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cvet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́стый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ástyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветастый.html>цвета́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cvetástyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)цвета́стее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)цвета́стей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>colorful, gaudy, garish</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветник.html>цветни́к</a> (22341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cvet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ни́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ník</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветник.html>цветни́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cvetník</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветник.html>цветника́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветник.html>цветники́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветник.html>цветнико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flower garden, parterre, flowerbed</li>
<li>a bevy of beautiful women
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:цветник.html>цветни́к</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on popál v nastojáščij <b>cvetník</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he is a thorn among roses</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cvet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cvet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цвето́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cvetók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flower <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">flowering part of a plant</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цвето́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cvetók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цвето́в</a></b>)

***цветущий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветущий.html>цвету́щий</a> (7615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветущий.html>цвету́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cvetúščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цвести.html>цвести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cvestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цветущий.html>цвету́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">cvetúščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>blooming, blossoming, flowering</li>
<li><i>(person)</i> blooming, in one's prime
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:цветущий.html>цвету́щий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>cvetúščij</b> vid</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he looks fine/blooming [in the pink (of health)]; he is a picture of health</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:цветущий.html>цвету́щая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:девушка.html>де́вушка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>cvetúščaja</b> dévuška</i> ― <span class="e-translation">girl in the full bloom of youth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
